    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

  <span id="freeText2746562038994783439" style="display:none">When Bobby Pendragon first arrives on the tropical world of Ibara, he finds paradise. There is beauty all around and the people of Ibara are blissfully happy. It's not long before Bobby discovers, however, that they are also blissfully...oblivious.<br /><br />The leaders of Ibara are keeping a devastating secret from their people, one that gives Saint Dane all the opportunity he needs to launch his final assault on Halla.<br /><br />While Bobby struggles to learn the truth in time to thwart Saint Dane, Courtney Chetwynde desperately searches for Mark Diamond. On the heels of a shocking tragedy, Mark has disappeared. Worse, he seems to be under Saint Dane's influence. It's up to Courtney to find Mark and stop him from making a grave mistake that could change the future of all existence.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer132830568" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11022035385867903814">The Pilgrims of Rayne (Pendragon, #8), D.J. MacHale<br/>The Pilgrims of Rayne is the eighth book in D. J. MacHale's Pendragon series. On October 17, 2006.<br/>Bobby and Courtney arrive on Third Earth only to find that it has changed quite noticeably. Patrick, the local Traveler, arrives and takes them to the library to find out about their friend Mark, whom they believe is on First Earth. Startlingly, information pertaining to Mark originates from both First Earth and Second Earth. Both sources tell of hi</span>
  <span id="freeText11022035385867903814" style="display:none">The Pilgrims of Rayne (Pendragon, #8), D.J. MacHale<br />The Pilgrims of Rayne is the eighth book in D. J. MacHale's Pendragon series. On October 17, 2006.<br />Bobby and Courtney arrive on Third Earth only to find that it has changed quite noticeably. Patrick, the local Traveler, arrives and takes them to the library to find out about their friend Mark, whom they believe is on First Earth. Startlingly, information pertaining to Mark originates from both First Earth and Second Earth. Both sources tell of him disappearing. In the flume, on First Earth November 1, 1937, Courtney and Bobby run into a dado (a type of android) in ragged clothing. Bobby tells Courtney to escape while he fights it off. Soon the dado backs into the tunnel and into an oncoming train. The dado is torn in half. Bobby takes the pieces to the flume and sends it back to Quillan. Then Bobby goes to First Earth to find Mark but he knows that Ibara needs him so he goes there and leaves Courtney behind. ...<br />عنوان: پندراگن: کتاب هشتم: جنگجویان راینه؛ نویسنده: دی.جی. مک هیل؛ مترجم: حسین شهرابی؛ مشخصات نشر: تهران، تندیس، 1393، در 622 ص، شابک: 9786001821158؛ موضوع: داستانهای ماجراجویانه از نویسندگان امریکایی - سده 21 م<br />آنگاه که «بابی پندراگن»، به دنیای استوایی: «ایبارا»، می‌رسد، می‌بیند که آن‌جا بهشت برین است. هرچه تلاش می‌کند، بفهمد نقطه‌ ی ضعف این قلمرو زیبا و دلپذیر، چیست، می‌بیند که مردمان «ایبارا» همگی غرق در نعمت هستند. او باز هم جستجو می‌کند، و بسیار زود پی می‌برد، که مردمان «ایبارا» در نادانی به سر میبرند. رهبران «ایبارا»، رازی مهم را، از مردمانشان پنهان می‌کنند؛ رازی که بی‌ شک، فرصتی به «سنت‌ دین» می‌دهد، تا آخرین حمله‌ ی بزرگش را، بر ضد «هالا»، ترتیب بدهد. «بابی» با تمام توان، می‌خواهد از راز قلمرو، سر دربیاورد، و با «سنت‌ دین» مقابله کند. «کورتنی چتویند»، به دنبال «مارک» است. «مارک» ناپدید شده، و با کارهایش او را نگران کرده است، و از همه بدتر، انگار از «سنت‌ دین» فرمان می‌گیرد. «کورتنی» باید به هر قیمتی، جلوی «مارک» را بگیرد، و نگذارد او، آینده‌ ی کائنات را، زیر و زبر کند. نبردهای این کتاب بیش از آنچه تا کنون خوانده‌ اید، خشن و تلخ‌ است. فریب بهشت «راینه» را نخورید؛ لا به‌ لای واژه‌ های این کتاب دوزخی بنشسته است. ا. شربیانی</span>
  <a data-text-id="11022035385867903814" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6572965338235222414">I do not understand why more people haven't read this series. It is hands down one of the best and most action packed fantasy stories I've ever read. I know it's an older series and that's probably part of the reason, as well as the fact that like Harry Potter, the first couple of books start out as almost middle grade, but as the books progress it definitely dips into YA.<br/><br/>I love every single character introduced in the story. Saint Dane is one of my favorite villains ever written. The concept an</span>
  <span id="freeText6572965338235222414" style="display:none">I do not understand why more people haven't read this series. It is hands down one of the best and most action packed fantasy stories I've ever read. I know it's an older series and that's probably part of the reason, as well as the fact that like Harry Potter, the first couple of books start out as almost middle grade, but as the books progress it definitely dips into YA.<br /><br />I love every single character introduced in the story. Saint Dane is one of my favorite villains ever written. The concept and premise of Halla and that the universe it split into ten different worlds called territories is one of the most intriguing concepts I've ever come across in fantasy literature. I just love everything about it and want to scream about this series to everyone who has never heard of or read it.<br /><br />That all being said, this book alone was probably the most action packed one yet. I love the new traveler, and I love seeing old faces brought back into play. The plot twist revealed near the middle of this is a big one. So many twists and turns in this story alone and we still have two books left.<br /><br />Hobey ho, let's go.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3690996469733046762">I love how this series, like other really good YA literature, grows along with its protagonist and its readers, getting progressively darker and more intense with each installment. Because there's no doubt that this is a heavy adventure.<br/><br/>Feeling harried and desperate after his loss on Quillan, Bobby and Courtney are torn. On one hand, they desperately need to find their friend Mark, who may have changed the future and allied with Saint Dane. But on the other hand, Saint Dane is targeting the terr</span>
  <span id="freeText3690996469733046762" style="display:none">I love how this series, like other really good YA literature, grows along with its protagonist and its readers, getting progressively darker and more intense with each installment. Because there's no doubt that this is a heavy adventure.<br /><br />Feeling harried and desperate after his loss on Quillan, Bobby and Courtney are torn. On one hand, they desperately need to find their friend Mark, who may have changed the future and allied with Saint Dane. But on the other hand, Saint Dane is targeting the territory of Ibara as his next and possibly most important conquest. So Bobby and Courtney make the difficult decision to split the duties.<br /><br />While Courtney meets up with Gunny's acolyte on First Earth, the hilariously clever Dodger, to search for Mark and stop him, Bobby heads to Ibara, a tropical island paradise where dark secrets are being kept. With only the help of the rebellious teenage Traveler Siry, Bobby is about to get some serious news tossed on him. Because nothing on Ibara is what it seems, and the mysteries behind it have staggering implications on the battle for Halla. And in order to put an end to the conflict once and for all, Bobby may have to make the biggest sacrifice he's ever been faced with. It's all coming to a head.<br /><br />With both plotlines packed with action, twists, and intense choices and revelations, this is the true lead-in novel to this series' finale. I still love its characters, even Saint Dane, who is such an incredible villain becuase of how terrifyingly clever and callous he is. I am so glad I have the next one ready, because MacHale knows how to hook a reader!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12442926235166891431">Goodness gracious, I don’t know what I was expecting when I started this book, but it certainly wasn’t what I got. What I got was much, much better than I ever could have hoped for.<br/><br/>From start to finish, this book was a complete and total mind-fuck and there was a new twist every other chapter it seemed. It’s starting to get crazy, everything is coming to fruition slowly and more and more questions are arising and I am so excited to read the last two books of this series.<br/><br/>As soon as Bobby decided </span>
  <span id="freeText12442926235166891431" style="display:none">Goodness gracious, I don’t know what I was expecting when I started this book, but it certainly wasn’t what I got. What I got was much, much better than I ever could have hoped for.<br /><br />From start to finish, this book was a complete and total mind-fuck and there was a new twist every other chapter it seemed. It’s starting to get crazy, everything is coming to fruition slowly and more and more questions are arising and I am so excited to read the last two books of this series.<br /><br />As soon as Bobby decided to part ways at the beginning, I knew it was going to be a crazy ride on both sides and I was absolutely right. It’s like starting at the two sides of the Matterhorn ride and wondering which bobsled will reach the bottom first.<br /><br />SO MUCH happened in this book, and it was hard to keep track of everything that happened from start to finish in this book. There was so much character development for Bobby, for Courtney, we finally got to know Dodger and I absolutely love him, and even for Mark. It’s been awesome to see how everyone is growing up and how everything is changing as the series goes.<br /><br />Bobby made some tough choices in this book, especially towards the end, and I am quite excited to see how everything turns out over the course of the last two books. I am so stoked for this series.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer43528255" class="readable"

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17138979444801030079">When Bobby first finds himself on the territory of Ibara, he wonders why Saint Dane would want to 're-build' this territory...it seemed so perfect. However, he soon learns that the leaders of Rayne are keeping one huge secret from the villagers ~ their past. Since he can't find answers on Rayne without being discovered, Bobby teams up with Siry, the last Traveler from Ibara, and his group, the Jakills. After hijacking a ship, Bobby and the Jakills travel to the nearest place on a map that Siry h</span>
  <span id="freeText17138979444801030079" style="display:none">When Bobby first finds himself on the territory of Ibara, he wonders why Saint Dane would want to 're-build' this territory...it seemed so perfect. However, he soon learns that the leaders of Rayne are keeping one huge secret from the villagers ~ their past. Since he can't find answers on Rayne without being discovered, Bobby teams up with Siry, the last Traveler from Ibara, and his group, the Jakills. After hijacking a ship, Bobby and the Jakills travel to the nearest place on a map that Siry had acquired. That place was called "Rubity" on the (very*100) old map. Ring any bells? Anyhow....as usual, Bobby learns of Saint Danes plan while Siry, (who doesn't believe in the Traveler business,) learns the horror of Saint Dane. Fortunately, Bobby and Siry manage to escape, but unfortunately, they are the only ones that remained alive after witnessing Saint Dane's insanity. When they get back to Ibara, they do the only thing they can; Reveal the past to the people of Rayne.</span>

<div id="review_3264022288" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3264022288" />
    <a title="Deviki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2484174-deviki"><img alt="Deviki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1311927680p2/2484174.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3264022288?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deviki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deviki" href="/user/show/2484174-deviki">Deviki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=books-i-enjoyed-reading">books-i-enjoyed-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=young-adult-books">young-adult-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=white_men_boy">white_men_boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=series_books">series_books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=diversity_mixed">diversity_mixed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=alien_spacetravel_planets">alien_spacetravel_planets</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=time_travel-or_time_jump">time_travel-or_time_jump</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=science_fiction">science_fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2484174-deviki?shelf=dystopian_world">dystopian_world</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3264022288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7849705581208810003">My immediate reaction, after reading this book............<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1570132473ra/28240203.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Honestly, why don't many people know about this series? It's frustrating because this is an AWESOME FANTASTIC adventure science fiction book !! And I really wish it had a cult following. It has perfect dynamic, diversity and science fiction world. <br/><br/>This book was action packed from the start till the end. And OMG! so many twist and reveals...... Some painful, some so bloody confusing and some shocking. This book had it all. One thing I not</span>
  <span id="freeText7849705581208810003" style="display:none">My immediate reaction, after reading this book............<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1570132473ra/28240203.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Honestly, why don't many people know about this series? It's frustrating because this is an AWESOME FANTASTIC adventure science fiction book !! And I really wish it had a cult following. It has perfect dynamic, diversity and science fiction world. <br><br>This book was action packed from the start till the end. And OMG! so many twist and reveals...... Some painful, some so bloody confusing and some shocking. This book had it all. One thing I notice about this series is how character development plays into the book, Bobby matures from book to book while the secondary traveler matures throughout their first book and then after their first appearance. <br><br>This series is getting darker and confusing and deliciously mysterious the more you read it. Only two books left :( Already, I'm starting to dread coming to the end of the saga. <br><br>I admit, I left this series for quite sometime because I was waiting until I could find the rest of the book. Thank god I already had the next two book ready at hand. <br><br>******MAJOR SPOILERS ALERT**********<br><br><br>The story starts of with Bobby and Courtney trying to find out what had happened to Mark and how he had cause a chain of change reaction to Second Earth technology. They arrive on Third Earth and found that the technology has affected there too, in creepy way that is....Patrick, the 3rd Earth Traveler help them find some clue on what happened to Mark, and with his help they figure out that he is in 1st Earth but there isn't much information to go on other then the fact he disappears suddenly in 1st Earth shortly after, so the duo travel to first earth to stop Mark from introducing the technology, but they were attacked by dados in rags ??? First weird clue right there!!<br><br>I don't know how I would have reacted if I had to stay behind to help stop Mark or Saint Dane in 1st Earth...alone. I admit Courtney is very brave! but she was also lucky she had Dodger with her. I understand why she was suspicious and tried to avoid Dodger at first, I mean I would too, Saint Dane could be anyone. Can't take the risk (again). At first, I wasn't sure if Bobby leaving Courtney behind was a good idea, especially after leaving her with such a heavy responsibility, but then again, I understand he can't help it. I felt bad for Bobby. <br><br>I felt even worse for him after he arrived in Ibara, dude did not come in with style. I really felt like Bobby is always the 80's and 90's action hero that gets beaten up badly before taking a stand. Those bees dayum!! Ibara is basically your Caribbean vacation island with enough modern technology to uplift it from total under developed civilization. It has a balanced mix of both modern and traditional living. <br><br>While everything looks peaceful and in harmony, there is something amiss, nobody seem to question anything. Also they are afraid of outsiders or more specifically "Flighters". Here is where we meet Siry, wow this dude was an arrogant "street" wise teen and the town trouble-maker. Unfortunately for Bobby, Siry is Remudi's son, Ibara's new traveler. <br><br>At first, I don't know what to make of Siry, he seem like a typical teenage trouble maker but after learning about why he and his crew the Jackills are behaving the way they are. I felt like his action could be justified, although, Siry your attitude was annoying as hell. I mean, their mission was honorable but they were not executed properly, so they come off as annoying brats. Sure, they have plans, tactic and passion, but they don't have proper skill or enough skill. Their fighting skill was laughable, I admit I wasn't expecting that at all LOL !!!<br><br>The thing about Bobby in this book, he doesn't have a direct path to guide him, like in other territory, Bobby knows who to trust and has help to understand the "situation" faced by them in that territory, In Ibara, Bobby was making decisions based on instinct even though some of them was questionable, especially after he agrees to join the Jakills to steal a ship and set off to find the truth. I mean, because Ibara's very own traveler has no clue what is going on, he as a mission but that's just it, so for Bobby like it or not, had to play along. <br><br>Oh...... Rubity city, whoaaaa that was not what I was expecting, while Bobby was explaining in his journal, I was starting to wonder if they were walking into a trap. I mean, I totally didn't make the connection until Bobby took note of what Twig said. Even I didn't notice that until Bobby pointed it out! The whole chaos that took place right after was heartbreaking and shocking. Aja Killian while a smart-mouth was still a legend in her own right, gosh she is an incredible character. I really admire her for that, I think she is my 3rd favorite traveler after Loor. <br><br>Saint Dane was waiting for them at the abandoned Lifelight pyramid. <br><br>Did you notice a trend in this book, I mean did Bobby, Courtney or Mark notice that Saint Dane take great lengths to confuse and spill just enough information to rile Bobby up ?<br>But did they notice that he always wants Bobby to know what he is going to do or wants to do ? Like he wants to provoke Bobby, pushing Bobby to make haste decisions ?<br><br>I think Bobby realize it (somehow) but sometimes, Bobby does get overwhelmed with emotion, he kind of forgets to take a step back. <br><br>Oh gosh, this Saint Dane, always plays dirty doesn't he? I mean, that dude is world class manipulator, And he is set on destroying Veelox's second turning point. Dude, give it a rest, you won the first time and now still wants to make sure it stays that way.....seriously he needs a new hobby LOL. <br><br>I wanted to smack The Tribunal and salute them at the same time, they followed Aja's directive diligently <i>(too diligently, mind you)</i> but I felt like they could have eased up on it after 300 years, because the people were so void of any knowledge of their p[ast and they seriously lack defense......so much so that they don't even know how to fight.<br><br>Now we understand why Bobby came to Veelox during this time period, the turning point was the pilgrimage mission. They were finally ready to set out to the rest of the Veelox, but lookie who comes to kill that even before it starts ??? <br><br>Right after this revelation, Bobby was already making dangerous and questionable decisions to save Ibara, he was breaking his own rule. I wasn't so thrilled about it but looking at the situation Ibara was in. It was either break the rule or watch Veelox crush and burn AGAIN .......<br><br>I admit, I was so excited when Bobby yelled Zadaa into the flume. I mean, Loor was mentioned in almost every chapter in this book and I was hoping he would meet her. But I was disappointed that he avoided her like a plague. He "borrowed" a dygo and made a cringe worthy hole in the flume <i> (I wonder if Loor is going to kick his arse when she found out)</i>, then in Denduron in order to unearth the explosive tak. <i>(I wonder if finding the tak again will set another war in Denduron)</i>. Oh I like Alder a lot, I always felt like he was one of the Traveler that was willing to help always Bobby even if he had doubts, such a gentle teddy bear knight warrior :) And finally from Quillan, Bobby gets the dado-killing rods for extra protection, yeah Bobby was breaking all kind of rules here. <br><br>After they discuss their plan of defense and attack with The Tribunal, I felt like they might have a wining chance. In the meantime, Courtney and Dougher was having their side of the adventure. Oh gosh, I was super confused after listening to Mark's reaction to Courtney's beseech. I wasn't sure Mark could be trusted especially after he showed his parents was there with him on the ship. <br><br>I thought he made the deal with the devil, but thank god Mark was a smart guy and he quickly started having doubts about his theory and reasoning. I was scared that either Mark or Dodger was going to ended up dead because of the tiny news article Courtney found in 1st Earth. Anything to "stop" Mark could also mean fatal. <br><br>I love that we were reading chapter after chapter of both type of adventure, one with Bobby and Siry and the other one with Courtney and Dougher. Oh! I also notice another thing, Saint Dane is not just very violent with Bobby, he seem to have same treatment for Courtney as well. Dude, don't give a dayum if either of them died. I'm not going to elaborate here on the story because you have to read it to FEEL IT. I hate to admit this but, Saint Dane was becoming very scary in the last few books, especially after Zadaa. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1586793770ra/29286384.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Why did Bobby had to do that at the end? I felt really really bad for him. Gosh he was truly desperate to save Hala, that he trapped himself and Saint Dane in Ibara. I was conflicted with his action, I wanted to scream at him!! I felt like Bobby made a huge mistake ! In this book, Bobby seem quite defeated, like he was giving up...tired. <br><br>At the end, <i>(for the first time Saint Dane got his own POV)</i> Saint Dane had said long ago, Denduron would be the first territory to fall, I guess it happened the moment Bobby went back to unearth the long "lost" tak. I think it unintentionally (on Bobby's part) reset a chain of event in Denduron, unbeknownst to him. I guess Siry was right to doubt Bobby's decision. <br><br>Did I know "she" was Nevva Winter the whole time ? No, not really..... although I did expect Nevva to be involved in Ibara from the start. <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7849705581208810003" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5836046-kailey-booksformks?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1396263700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5012181738424306128">Every single book in this series is amazing! Every chapter blows me away. I never know what is going to happen next, and I'm always surprised by the impossible plot twists.<br/><br/>This time Bobby is fighting to save the territory of Ibara and the small village of Rayne. Ibara seems like a peaceful paradise, but this territory holds a secret that even Bobby will have trouble with, and the Traveler from Ibara wants nothing to do with him. The evil Saint Dane is up to his clever tricks again, but Bobby is </span>
  <span id="freeText5012181738424306128" style="display:none">Every single book in this series is amazing! Every chapter blows me away. I never know what is going to happen next, and I'm always surprised by the impossible plot twists.<br /><br />This time Bobby is fighting to save the territory of Ibara and the small village of Rayne. Ibara seems like a peaceful paradise, but this territory holds a secret that even Bobby will have trouble with, and the Traveler from Ibara wants nothing to do with him. The evil Saint Dane is up to his clever tricks again, but Bobby is having trouble telling right from wrong, and there is no way to figure out how to counteract Saint Dane's evil plans.<br />While Bobby is fighting for Ibara, Mark and Courtney are stranded in the past on First Earth in the 1930s. Mark is in danger of being murdered at sea, and it's up to Courtney to stop the invention of the robotic dados.<br /><br />It amazes me how all the story lines and characters from different worlds come together so beautifully in all these books. It's like this intricate web of plot and people that draws in so neatly; it leaves me in awe of the scope of the writing. Simply brilliant!<br /><br />I love how we are dragged back and forth between dizzying triumph and devastating defeat countless times in each book. Just when I think the heroes have won, there comes a terrible plot twist that tears out my heart, and keeps me reading into the wee hours.<br /><br />Bobby is such a wonderful main character. I feel all his ups and downs. I cheer for him, and weep with him. He's so deliciously human, making foolish mistakes, feeling impossible combinations of emotion, and through it all he's so wonderfully heroic. I simply adore him!<br /><br />Can't wait to read the rest of this series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5012181738424306128" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5510840350470210754" style="display:none">"The Pilgrims of Rayne" was another wonderful entry into the Pendragon series by D.J. MacHale. it is a fantastic adventure novel in which the main character Bobby Pendragon once again has been sent to a brand new territory of Ibara, a perfect paradise island, to stop the evil saint Dane before he causes more mayhem. Meanwhile on Earth one Courtney Chetwynde is trying to stop Mark Dimond before he brings about the end of all Halla. This book was fantastic, its writing was really organized, but still easy to read. The development, characteristics, and personality of the characters made it really fun to read, a great book. The main issue I have with the book is the length, over 500 pages is a little longer than my liking. That aside a great book with all the drama, intrigue, and adventure you could need.</span>

<div id="review_2024289830" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2024289830" />
    <a title="Nina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20966982-nina"><img alt="Nina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1496991380p2/20966982.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2024289830?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nina" href="/user/show/20966982-nina">Nina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781416914174" href="/book/show/2891264-the-pilgrims-of-rayne">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2024289830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11593692783201465931">So far my absolute favourite of the series (I've yet to read <i>Soldiers of Halla</i> at this point). But, TLDR, it's got a simple yet deceptively complex territory, great story flow, a great set of new characters, mystery, and a childish flair.<br/><br/>I loved the territory. Ibara is beautiful, and simple. Pendragon doesn't spend too much time dissecting this territory as there's not much to dissect. But there's a much bigger mystery out there, one that's link to the mystery of the Travelers, and I found that </span>
  <span id="freeText11593692783201465931" style="display:none">So far my absolute favourite of the series (I've yet to read <i>Soldiers of Halla</i> at this point). But, TLDR, it's got a simple yet deceptively complex territory, great story flow, a great set of new characters, mystery, and a childish flair.<br /><br />I loved the territory. Ibara is beautiful, and simple. Pendragon doesn't spend too much time dissecting this territory as there's not much to dissect. But there's a much bigger mystery out there, one that's link to the mystery of the Travelers, and I found that to be more interesting; taking away with it the tedium of the story formula. Siry (the Traveler from Ibara) and the Jakills (his friends), are an amazing set of cast, eventhough barely established. Would've loved to have more Loque and Twig in the story. Of all the territory side-characters, Ibara has the best, and the homiest feeling. (<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And I think Pendragon agrees considering how he decided to make Ibara his retirement resort  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>). The mystery, was amazing. The reveal was great. I can't get over it. (<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I mean, holywow Ibara is part of Veelox?? Years in the future? Mind-blowing. Aja Killian is amazing, btw  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>). The hunt for the turning point felt less of an importance than it was solving the mystery of Ibara, and it's great because as I've said, the turning point thing was getting tedious. What better way than to hide it behind a wall of mystery and seemingly childish adventures?<br /><br />The battle of philosophy and wits peaks with this book, between Saint Dane and Bobby. You'll find yourself screaming at Bobby for his recklessness (no matter how hard he tries to justify himself) and, if you're like me, you'll realise that Bobby is probably one of your least favourite characters.<br /><br />Back to Earth, we have Courtney on the hunt for Mark. While the pacing for Ibara was slower, things kick up hard in this segment of the story. Courtney and Dodger (First Earth acolyte) are constantly running and looking for Mark, while trying to solve the mystery that seems to surround Mark Dimond. What does Saint Dane and Nevva want with Mark? Why push him this far? How is he important to the fate of, not just First Earth, but Second AND Third Earth? DUN DUN DUNNN<br /><br />Loved this book. Dived right into <i>Raven Rise</i> immediately after.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11593692783201465931" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Maberan Potato" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47565421-maberan-potato"><img alt="Maberan Potato" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541355935p2/47565421.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2127631519" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11429851504277528328">WHY COULDN'T THEY ALL BE THIS GOOD<br/><br/>Seriously if I'd never read those books as a child, I would've given up at the second book, maybe fourth if I were fifteen. Either something happened or the author is just on fire!<br/><br/>So Bobby. Bobby is getting reaaaally fun. He's cold, down-to-earth and kind of a pessimistic smart-ass. Aka great. His story was nice, although Rayne wasn't all that interesting, they didn't waste time anywhere where they shouldn't be and it flowed pretty well. OH AND THE TWISTS THERE </span>
  <span id="freeText11429851504277528328" style="display:none">WHY COULDN'T THEY ALL BE THIS GOOD<br /><br />Seriously if I'd never read those books as a child, I would've given up at the second book, maybe fourth if I were fifteen. Either something happened or the author is just on fire!<br /><br />So Bobby. Bobby is getting reaaaally fun. He's cold, down-to-earth and kind of a pessimistic smart-ass. Aka great. His story was nice, although Rayne wasn't all that interesting, they didn't waste time anywhere where they shouldn't be and it flowed pretty well. OH AND THE TWISTS THERE ARE SO MANY TWISTY TWISTS YES. I remember them all tho so I was not surprised.<br /><br />AND SAINT DANE IS GETTING BETTER. GOOD. He's got more of a goal than EVIL MWAHAHAHA and him and Bobby have like history and chemistry and just??? YES???<br /><br />So Ibara was good. Thumbs up, keep it going, I'm proud of you.<br /><br />Courtney tho.... like, it was fine and stressful and good, but like.... Mark is so dumb. OK, Courtney says something that sounds like a lie. But wouldn't you try to PROVE to her that what she's saying is indeed a lie, because she's still your friend who stuck with you through highs and lows??? Like she says one thing that's not true and Mark is immediately like 'Goodbye Courtney, let me leave you, my best friend, alone while I go with my childhood bully whom you claim is our worst enemy and a Traveler whose territory collapsed and that I did not read the end to, and also say that Bobby, our #1 best friend in the universe, is wrong because he is. Nya.'<br /><br />Like it was just so ??? MARK YOU ARE NOT DUMB. It really seems to me like the author had good ideas, like having <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Courtney hold Mark at gunpoint, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but didn't know how to get there, so the characters suffer from mild Ooc from time to time and it's really distracting.<br /><br />But yes this was good. Bobby is getting very nice. I like him. My one complaint would be there's a scene that's not at all that dramatic compared to whatever Bobby's seen and yet he's all 'I almost cried and gave up right there what is life' and it was reeaally weird.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11429851504277528328" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7649753259022119465" style="display:none"> Many kids get bored about the the fact to read a big chapter book such as Pendragon “The Pilgrims of Rayne” but It all changed for me at least when I started this whole series or you would say it the Pendragon series. The most Impressive thing I Thought about this whole book is how the author was able to hook people into reading the first book such as myself. Other reasons why I liked this book so much is how descriptive the author wrote this book. I like the fact like Harry Potter the book slowly progress to when they are adults or more mature. If you didn’t read this book you are missing in all the drama, action and the suspense. <br /><br />I thought Pendragon series so far was one of the best series of books I have ever read so far.<br />One of my reasons why I think that is that the author makes the plot expand over certain amount of time of their life, so it almost feels like you're living through the the main character's life in the story like Harry Potter. Other reasons is that the way the author wrote these characters like they were actually real and not just story and the way the author used the different kind of English slang. The last reason why I think this book was one of best book ever is that the book slowly get more Intense by each book which makes the readers want to read the rest of the series. These are my reasons why I like the book and the series of Pendragon.<br /></span>

Boy oh boy was that a decision. <br /><br />This series has really kept me on my toes. I’ve never read a YA series that is as complex and dark as this one. The way the author transforms Bobby’s character (and everyone else’s) over time is unparalleled. <br /><br />This book made me realize just how deceptive and cunning the antagonist is, and Bobby doesn’t “win” every book. Things are never finished in a clean cut way. No, things get more complicated as time progresses. <br /><br />I already ordered the last two books, so I’ll eagerly await their arrival. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vOXpHzEmr/0r+yXaCR6GbPwQYIdwihD4Mv1yrtIzxWWFh1OjURz5RIusYsnw7cv7Ss1sKZpMks7d+WrF+caI/A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AaXJhCLVkyhP+5YLdLHXcL1Tc3Np+UM3C4l0+5VFzQg4x3M4Qu/Fke+s0RiNQprnC45/3YM/wQHkjWyQvrCAkQ==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/74046.D_J_MacHale">About D.J. MacHale</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/74046.D_J_MacHale"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1418514923p3/74046.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/74046.D_J_MacHale">D.J. MacHale
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
2,018
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13632361975989955377">D.J. MacHale is a writer, director, executive producer and creator of several popular television series and movies.<br/><br/>He was raised in Greenwich, CT and graduated from Greenwich High School. While in school, he had several jobs including collecting eggs at a poultry farm, engraving sports trophies and washing dishes in a steakhouse...in between playing football and running track. D.J. then attended N</span>
  <span id="freeText13632361975989955377" style="display:none">D.J. MacHale is a writer, director, executive producer and creator of several popular television series and movies.<br /><br />He was raised in Greenwich, CT and graduated from Greenwich High School. While in school, he had several jobs including collecting eggs at a poultry farm, engraving sports trophies and washing dishes in a steakhouse...in between playing football and running track. D.J. then attended New York University where he received a BFA in film production.<br /><br />His filmmaking career began in New York where he worked as a freelance writer/director, making corporate videos and television commercials. He also taught photography and film production.<br /><br />D.J. broke into the entertainment business by writing several ABC Afterschool Specials. After moving to Los Angeles, he made the fulltime switch from informational films, to entertainment. As co-creator of the popular Nickelodeon series: Are You Afraid of the Dark?, he produced all 91 episodes over 8 years. He wrote and directed many of the episodes including the CableAce nominated The Tale of Cutter's Treasure starring Charles S. Dutton. He was nominated for a Gemini award for directing The Tale of the Dangerous Soup starring Neve Campbell.<br /><br />D.J. also wrote and directed the movie Tower of Terror for ABC's Wonderful World of Disney which starred Kirsten Dunst and Steve Guttenberg. The Showtime series Chris Cross was co-created, written and produced by D.J. It received the CableAce award for Best Youth Series.<br /><br />D.J. co-created and produced the Discovery Kids series Flight 29 Down for which he writes all the episodes and directs several. His work on Flight 29 Down has earned him both Writers Guild of America and Directors Guild of America award nominations.<br /><br />Other notable writing credits include the classic ABC Afterschool Special titled Seasonal Differences; the pilot for the long-running PBS/CBS series Ghostwriter; and the HBO series Encyclopedia Brown, Boy Detective for which he received a CableAce nomination for writing.<br /><br />In print, D.J. has co-written the book The Tale of the Nightly Neighbors, based on his own teleplay and penned the poetic adaptation of the classic Norwegian folk tale East of the Sun and West of the Moon.<br /><br />The book series: Pendragon - Journal of an Adventure through Time and Space marks D.J.'s first turn as a novelist. He plans for this series of Young Adult adventures to span a total of 10 books.<br /><br />D.J. lives in Southern California with his wife Evangeline and daughter Keaton. They are avid backpackers, scuba divers and skiers. Rounding out the household are a Golden Retriever, Maggie; and a Kitten, Kaboodle. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13632361975989955377" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
